### Sr Manager Role Gate Pattern (Session 47)
- **5 UI role gates updated** (commit `d5ddc36`) to include `hasRole('Sr Manager')` alongside `isAdmin() || hasRole('Manager')`.
- Affected locations: Set Parts Status button (card template), Schedule buttons (compact card, expanded mobile panel, standard card), `openPartsStatusModal()` guard.
- **`isManagerOrAbove()` helper recommended** — consolidate the scattered 3-way check into one function. Currently 5+ locations with `isAdmin() || hasRole('Manager') || hasRole('Sr Manager')`.
- Root cause: `Sr Manager` is a distinct role string from `Manager`. The `staffRoleMap` maps `sr_manager` → `'Sr Manager'` (not `'Manager'`), so Kevin's `userRoles` array was `['Sr Manager']` — which didn't match `hasRole('Manager')`.

### Template Literal Parser Bomb
- Never put `</script>` inside a template literal assigned to `.innerHTML` — HTML parser closes the outer script block. Move JS to named functions and wire via `onclick`/`onchange` attributes.

### Spanish Toggle
- `t(str)` — English string IS the key. Emoji must be INSIDE the `t()` call: `${t('🖨️ Print Label')}` not `🖨️ ${t('Print Label')}`. DB values stay English.

### Git & Deployment
- `gh` CLI not available in sandbox — use `git` directly.
- Workspace folder IS the git repo. **But NEVER `git push origin main` directly** — that predates the S79 pre-prod branch model and re-creates the Session 83 drift. Doc/checkpoint commits go to `pre-prod`; `main` only ever moves by fast-forward via the 🔒 Sync Gate. (Stale line caught by Class K, fixed S143.)
- Never push directly to GitHub during an active Claude session (causes branch divergence requiring `git reset --hard`).
- Always run `bash scripts/backup.sh` before `git push`.

### Work Order System
- Roland Shepard must be in `staff` table as `sr_manager` (NULL silo) for WO RLS to work. Future admins needing WO access also need a `staff` row.
- `_staffCache` loads async after initial render — `canManageSilo()` falls back to hardcoded email lists until cache loads (<1s in practice).
- **SERVICE_SILOS** array has 8 entries: repair, vroom, solar, roof, paint_body, chassis, detailing, truetopper.
- **REPAIR_TYPE_TO_SILO** maps repairType string → silo key (case-insensitive). **SILO_TO_REPAIR_TYPE** maps silo key → canonical label. Both defined immediately after SERVICE_SILOS const.
- `renderWorkOrderView` filters silos to RO's active services only. `addServiceToRO(roIndex, siloKey)` updates `repair_type` on the RO then opens Build WO form — keeps tile + modal in sync.
- **Chevron toggle:** `toggleWOTasks(tasksId, chevId)` — task divs hidden by default (`display:none`). Chevron only rendered when `siloTasks.length > 0`. `event.stopPropagation()` on Edit/Build button prevents chevron click bleed.
- **osascript file editing pattern:** Write Python to `/tmp/patch_xxx.py` using AppleScript `write s to fp` then `do shell script "python3 /tmp/patch_xxx.py"`. Never use inline `-c` with JS template literals (backticks/quotes/dollar signs cause parse failures).

### Supabase Pro Security (Session 28)
- Removed all anon write policies from 9 tables. Fixed `has_role`/`is_silo_manager` mutable search_path. Disabled new user signups.
- ✅ Anon INSERT/UPDATE on `time_logs` removed 2026-04-05 (checkin.html v1.28 now uses authenticated sessions).

### WO Task Templates (Session 30)
- `window._pendingTemplateTasks` — global used to pass task array from `saveWOTemplate()` to `commitSaveTemplate()`. Avoids embedding complex JSON in onclick attributes.
- Template overlays must use `z-index:100000` — WO modal is z-index:11000; anything lower renders behind it.
- `saveWOTemplate()` wraps body in `try { ... } catch(err) { ... }` — if the catch block is ever removed (e.g. debug cleanup), JS fails with "Missing catch or finally after try" and breaks the entire page.

### Modal Outside-Click Lock (Session 30)
- **New RO modal (`modalOverlay`)** and **Work Order modal (`workOrderOverlay`)** no longer close on outside click — the backdrop click handlers were removed to prevent data loss when techs accidentally click outside.
- View-only modals (photo lightbox, QR, dupe manager) still close on outside click — intentional, no data at risk.
- Close via ✕ button only on form modals.

### osascript / Python Patch Pattern (Session 30)
- For any file edit involving JS template literals, emoji, backticks, `${}`, or `\n`: write the Python patch to sandbox via `Write` tool → base64-encode with `Bash` → `osascript: do shell script "echo '...' | base64 -d > /tmp/patch.py && python3 /tmp/patch.py"`. Never use AppleScript inline string concatenation for complex JS content.

### GH#16 Manager Work List (Session 31)
- `manager_work_lists` table was created in a prior session with wrong schema (had `ro_supabase_id` NOT NULL instead of `ro_id`). Fixed by DROP + CREATE TABLE with correct columns.
- Supabase JS client name in this codebase is **`getSB()`** — NOT `supabaseClient`. All Supabase calls in worklist functions use `getSB().from(...)`.
- `addToWorkList` receives **`ro._supabaseId`** (UUID) as argument and uses `currentData.find()` to look up the RO — never pass array index from a sorted display list to a function that reads `currentData[]` (arrays differ after sort).
- Python Unicode escape `\u0001f4cb` is wrong for 📋 emoji (U+1F4CB). Use HTML entity `&#128203;` or Python `\U0001F4CB` (capital U, 8 hex digits). All emoji in patches should use HTML entities.
- `_initWorkListBtn()` must be both **defined** (function body) and **called** after staff cache loads. Check both when debugging button visibility.

### Training Guide PDFs (Session 33)
- **ReportLab Helvetica font does NOT support emoji** — any emoji character (🔧 🚗 📋 ✉️ etc.) renders as a solid black square. Always use plain text for PDF generation with ReportLab's built-in fonts.
- Both PDF and DOCX versions of training guides are maintained in `docs/`. PDF for distribution, DOCX for editing.
- Build scripts: `build_guide.py` (ReportLab PDF) and `build_guide_docx.py` (python-docx DOCX) in sandbox at `/sessions/sweet-relaxed-babbage/`. These are session-local only — not committed to the repo.

### Supabase Auth — New User Onboarding
- **New signups are disabled** (Session 28 security cleanup). Any new PRVS employee must be **invited** via Supabase → Authentication → Users → Invite User before they can use checkin.html or index.html.
- Symptom if missing: Google sign-in succeeds (name shows at bottom of page) but `signInWithIdToken()` fails silently → `supabaseSession` stays null → "Your session is not ready yet. Please sign out and sign back in."
- Hit by: Nik Polizzo (Session 33, fixed Session 34), Zak Wombles (Session 36, fixed). Remaining techs may still need invites.
- Riley Scott's work email is `solar@patriotsrvservices.com` (not `riley@`). Updated in MANAGER_EMAILS Session 35.

### GH#16 Sr Manager Silo Work Lists (Session 34)
- `service_silo TEXT` column on `manager_work_lists` — nullable. NULL for regular managers, silo key string for Sr Managers. **Migration must be run manually in Supabase SQL Editor.**
- `_workListActiveSilo` state var tracks which silo tab is selected in the sidebar panel.
- `_showSiloPickerForAdd()` creates a modal overlay (z-index:12500) for Sr Managers to pick a silo. Shows already-added silos as disabled green buttons.
- Same RO can be added to multiple silo lists — duplicate check is per-silo, not per-RO.
- `_renderWorkListSiloTabs()` called from `loadWorkList()` after data loads. Tabs always shown for Sr Manager lists, hidden for regular managers.
- `_workListActiveSilo` resets to null when switching managers via the picker dropdown.

### worklist-report.html (Session 34)
- Standalone admin-only report page at `/worklist-report.html`.
- Uses its own Supabase auth with `storageKey: 'prvs_report_auth'` (separate from index.html's `prvs_supabase_auth`).
- `repair_orders` column for date is `date_received` (NOT `date_in`). Days on lot uses `date_arrived || date_received` matching dashboard logic.
- `time_logs` column for tech email is `user_id` (NOT `tech_email`). Tech display name in `tech_name` column.
- Staff tiles show all active staff from `_allStaff`. Work list sections exclude users not in the `staff` table (i.e., admin-only users with no operational role).

### Work List Report Exclusion Rules (Session 52, v1.5+)
- **Testers = `staff.hourly_rate = 0`.** Treated as full exclusion from every report surface in `worklist-report.html`. Roland, Kevin, Sofia are all at `0.00`. Their staff row is kept intact (for rate lookup purposes) but their `time_logs` entries are filtered out at load in `applyReportExclusions()`. Their Staff Status tile does not render. Their manager accordion (if any) is suppressed.
- **Training ROs = `repair_orders.is_training = true`.** Added GH#24 in index.html v1.404. Filtered out at load in `applyReportExclusions()`: `_allROs`, `_allWorkLists`, `_allTimeLogs`, `_allActiveClockIns`, `_allTodayTimeLogs`, `_allAutoClosed`.
- **Both filters MUST run in sequence** after all loads finish. `applyReportExclusions()` is called in `loadAllData` at step 7 (after staff + ROs + time_logs are populated) — do not re-order this.
- **Adding a new data array** that feeds the report (future feature)? Add its filter line to `applyReportExclusions()` alongside the existing ones. Easy to forget and the data silently pollutes reports.
- **Subtle rule:** Sofia was added to `staff` mid-session (via Roland's SQL) at rate $0 so she counts as a tester. She's not in the main staff roster in this file — if she ever needs to be priced (i.e., she becomes operational), update her rate + remove her from `project_staff_testers.md` memory.

### GH#33 Phase 1 — UNIQUE Partial Index on time_logs (Session 53, 2026-04-21)
- **DB guarantee now:** `idx_time_logs_one_open_per_tech_ro` ensures a second open `time_logs` row for the same `(tech_email, ro_id)` is physically impossible. Any INSERT attempt returns 23505 unique_violation.
- **Partial predicate `WHERE clock_out IS NULL`** — closed rows are excluded from the index, so a tech can legitimately clock in → clock out → clock in again on the same RO. Do NOT remove the partial predicate.
- **Client-side expectations** (checkin.html v1.30):
  - `_clockInPending` is the authoritative in-flight guard. Don't use `setTimeout` debounce as a substitute — `_clockInPending` is reset in `finally {}` regardless of success/error path.
  - Button lock relies on `id="clockInBtn"` on the Clock In button. If rendering changes, preserve that ID or the lock fails silently.
  - Pre-INSERT SELECT guard + 23505 handler must BOTH remain — the SELECT prevents most cases, the 23505 handler catches the race-window remainder. Removing either reintroduces dupe risk.
  - `drainQueue()` dedup logic drops 23505-rejected queue items — don't change this to retry or queued items will stay forever.
- **Adding a new write path that inserts into `time_logs`?** Handle 23505 gracefully — catch the error code, re-sync state from the existing open row, show a friendly message. Don't let it bubble up as raw "duplicate key value violates unique constraint" to the user.
- **Phase 2 (not yet done):** systemic dedupe scan across ALL time_logs for historical rapid-fire patterns. Most ROs likely have Ignacio-style dupes lurking. Roland's Scott Kline RO cleanup Session 53 was manual + targeted. Deferred to post-baseline-collection window (~1 week).

### Auto-Logout Regime Change (Session 53, 2026-04-21) — 12h cap → 5 PM EOD
- **The 12h cap is gone.** `auto_close_stale_time_logs()` function was dropped. `auto-close-stale-time-logs` pg_cron unscheduled. Don't reintroduce — it inflated labor costs on the Work List Report (phantom 12h sessions from forgotten clock-outs).
- **New cron:** `close-open-time-logs-eod` (pg_cron job ID 8) runs `0 22 * * 1-5` (M-F 22:00 UTC = 5 PM CDT / 4 PM CST). Calls `close_open_time_logs_eod()` which sets `clock_out = NOW()` + `close_reason = 'auto_eod_5pm'` on any open session where `extended_at IS NULL OR extended_at < NOW() - interval '1 hour'`.
- **Weekend behavior:** no Saturday/Sunday run. Weekend work ends 2-3 PM per Roland's Q2 — weekend stragglers remain open until Monday's 5 PM cron (or tech clocks out manually). Accept the small drift.
- **Extension mechanism:** `time_logs.extended_at` column set by `twilio-webhook` when tech replies `YES`. Dormant pre-Twilio (always NULL → cron always fires).
- **DST caveat:** same as other pg_cron jobs — update UTC offset in November 2026 when CDT → CST.

### `close_reason` Values Reference (Session 53)
- `NULL` → normal tech-initiated clock_out.
- `'auto_eod_5pm'` → closed by the M-F 5 PM EOD cron. Surfaces as orange "5pm auto" badge in worklist-report audit.
- `'auto_eod_8h_recalc'` → retroactively rewritten from a prior 12h-cap close. Surfaces as gray "✓ 8h recalc" badge — data corrected, NOT a flag.
- `'auto_eod'` (legacy) → closed by the deprecated 12h cron. Should be ZERO new rows going forward; any still present were not yet rewritten. Surfaces as orange "12h auto" badge.
- `'tech_sms_reply'` → closed via SMS OUT/CLOCKOUT reply (Stage 2 post-Twilio).
- Report audit query uses `close_reason LIKE 'auto_%'`; rendering logic in worklist-report.html v1.9 maps each value to the right CSS class + badge label.

### GH#33 Rapid-Fire Clock-In Dupes — broader than originally thought
- **Session 52 first noted** Ignacio's 8-sec cluster (6 rows at 14:40:16-14:40:24) as an offline-queue replay pattern.
- **Session 53 found Mauricio has the same pattern at a different tempo:** 2 clock-ins 3 seconds apart at 13:00:42 and 13:00:45 on same RO/day. That's a simple double-tap (tech hit button, no visual feedback, hit again) — unrelated to the offline queue.
- **Two separate root causes** → one fix that covers both: a DB-level UNIQUE partial index `(tech_email, ro_id) WHERE clock_out IS NULL` that makes it physically impossible to have 2 open clock-ins for the same tech on the same RO. Paired with checkin.html button-lock + 23505 handling.
- **Manual Session 53 cleanup** on Scott Kline's RO only (5 Ignacio rapid-fire + 1 Mauricio 3-sec + 1 synthetic Ignacio over-written). Labor 28.25h → 19.02h. Other ROs likely have similar dupes lurking — Phase 2 dedupe scan will surface them.
- When writing the fix: DO the DB index FIRST. It's load-bearing and stops new dupes the moment it's created. Client changes harden UX but the index is the accuracy guarantee.
- **Don't delete `4a3040ce`-class synthetic rows wholesale** if a "real" clock-out sibling exists — prefer the one with the real `clock_out` over the `auto_eod_8h_recalc` row. That's exactly what happened on Ignacio 14:40:16 vs 14:40:26 during the manual cleanup.

### time-off.html v1.2 — Partial Day Design Notes (Session 62, 2026-04-30)
- **Self-service only:** Employee dropdown was removed from the request modal in v1.1. ALL roles (Tech, Manager, Admin) now submit for themselves only. Manager visibility is preserved on the view side (filter bar). Removing the dropdown required: deleting `loadStaff()` modal population block, removing the `isManagerOrAbove()` branch in `submitRequest()`, and deleting the stale `document.getElementById('modalEmployee').value = ''` line from `openRequestModal()` (element was gone — would throw a JS error).
- **`partial_hours` column MUST be in the SELECT:** `loadTimeOffData()` SELECT must include `partial_hours`. If it's omitted, `r.partial_hours` is always `undefined` — all calendar chips, list view chips, stat calculations, and `dayValue()` calls silently produce wrong output. The v1.0 SELECT did NOT include it; fixed in v1.2 before push.
- **`total_days` is a generated column:** It returns `end_date - start_date + 1` — always 1 for same-day partial requests. Rather than altering the generated column, the JS `dayValue(r)` helper overrides display: `if (r.partial_hours) return parseFloat(r.partial_hours) / 8; return parseFloat(r.total_days) || countDays(...)`. Day fraction is on an 8-hour workday basis.
- **Reason field reuses `notes` column:** No new DB column was added. The UI label changed from "Notes (optional)" → "Reason *" and it is now required for all requests (full + partial). The `notes` column in DB stays `notes` — backward compatible with existing rows.
- **`end` is forced to `start` for partial requests:** `submitRequest()` sets `end = start` on the partial path so `total_days` always generates as 1. No end-date field shown in the UI for partials.
- **16-option hours select:** 0.5h through 8.0h in 0.5h increments (16 `<option>` elements). Selecting "Partial Day" reveals the `#partialGroup` div with this select; selecting "Full Day" hides it.

### Supabase SQL Editor Gotcha — COMMENT string phrase patterns (Session 53)
- Pasted a single SQL block that concatenated DELETE + migration + COMMENT statements with long descriptive strings. The editor errored `42601 unterminated quoted string` at the `COMMENT ON COLUMN time_logs.close_reason IS '...'` line — even though my literal string was well-formed (balanced single-quotes, no embedded apostrophes).
- **Workaround:** split into smaller blocks AND drop the COMMENT statements entirely (they're documentation-only, not required for the migration to work). Three separate paste blocks ran clean.
- Unclear whether Supabase's dashboard parser has specific phrase-pattern allergies or whether the specific whitespace/linebreak mix in my paste did it. Safe move in future: keep inline SQL migrations COMMENT-lite, one schema change per paste.

### `time_logs.close_reason` Audit Column (Session 52, GH#32)
- `close_reason TEXT` added via `supabase/migrations/auto_logout_time_logs.sql`.
- Values: `NULL` = normal tech-initiated clock_out. `'auto_eod'` = closed by the nightly `auto_close_stale_time_logs()` cron at `clock_in + 12h`. Future values reserved: `'geofence_exit'`, `'admin_force'`.
- pg_cron job `auto-close-stale-time-logs` runs `0 2 * * *` (02:00 UTC = 9 PM CDT / 8 PM CST). Same DST offset caveat as the other jobs — update in November 2026.
- **To test manually:** `SELECT auto_close_stale_time_logs();` returns the count of rows closed. Safe to run as often as you want; idempotent.
- Function is `SECURITY DEFINER` with explicit `SET search_path = public` (S7 hygiene pattern).
- Report-side display: `worklist-report.html v1.7` highlights auto-closed sessions in orange inside Staff Status tiles. Tile-level color unchanged.

### Labor Load Chart — Per-Silo Attribution Nuance (Session 52, v1.4)
- An RO that appears on multiple silo lists (Sr Manager with a cross-silo RO) shows up as a **bar in each silo lane**, with the SAME total labor $ in both. Labor is not split across silos — we don't currently have a schema-supported way to attribute hours to a silo (would require a per-silo clock-in picker or a join from `time_logs` to `service_work_orders` and attribution to the active WO's silo at clock-in time).
- This is documented but flagged as sub-item (8) of the GH#31 "Finish Work List Reporting" major TODO. Revisit when Roland cares enough to diverge.

### Chart SELECT bug — urgency (Session 52, fixed v1.5)
- v1.4 shipped with `ro.urgency` referenced in `urgencyClass(ro)` but `urgency` was NOT in the `repair_orders` SELECT list. Effect: all bars rendered with the default gray top-border regardless of actual urgency. Silent bug — no error, just wrong visual.
- Fixed v1.5 by adding `urgency` to the SELECT. Lesson: when adding any new `ro.<field>` reference in rendering, grep the SELECT first. For future additions, sweep: `id, ro_id, customer_name, rv, repair_type, status, urgency, date_received, date_arrived, dollar_value, parking_spot, is_training`.

### Sandbox `.git/*.lock` Permission Trap (Session 52)
- The Cowork sandbox sometimes creates git lockfiles (`index.lock`, `HEAD.lock`, `refs/remotes/origin/main.lock`, `.git/objects/**/tmp_obj_*`) that the sandbox itself cannot unlink with `rm` — "Operation not permitted" on files it owns. Subsequent `git add`/`commit`/`push` then fail with "Another git process seems to be running" or "cannot lock ref 'HEAD'".
- **Canonical fix (one-liner for Roland's terminal):** `cd /Users/rolandshepard/rv-dashboard && find .git -name '*.lock' -delete && git add … && git commit -m "…" && git push origin main`. The `find -delete` clears ALL lock types in one pass — no need to iterate `rm` per-file.
- From the sandbox, `find .git -name '*.lock' -delete 2>/dev/null` as a preflight before `git add` usually works when paired in the same `&&` chain. But if a lock is recreated mid-chain (git add holds an index.lock, git commit tries again), hand off to Roland. Memory: `feedback_run_git_directly.md` has the full playbook.

### GH#30 Soft-Delete Architecture (Session 51, v1.409)
- `repair_orders.deleted_at TIMESTAMPTZ` + `deleted_by TEXT` — set by admin Delete RO action via Edit RO modal footer; cleared by Restore.
- `loadDataFromSupabase()` has **`.is('deleted_at', null)`** — NEVER remove. Soft-deleted ROs must not reach `currentData` or they'll show on the board.
- `scrub_soft_deleted_ros()` is a SECURITY DEFINER function scheduled via pg_cron job ID 6 (cron name `scrub-soft-deleted-ros`), daily `0 7 * * *` (07:00 UTC = 02:00 CDT). Cascades children explicitly (service_tasks via service_work_orders; then notes/parts/time_logs/audit_log/insurance_scans/manager_work_lists; then parent) so it doesn't rely on FK `ON DELETE CASCADE` which hasn't been audited on every table.
- Hard-delete path `hardDeleteROnow()` in index.html mirrors the same child-deletion ordering as `scrub_soft_deleted_ros()`. If the migration's scrub function changes ordering, update the JS to match — they must stay in sync or admin-initiated hard deletes will leak orphans that the nightly scrub can then never clean.
- **`audit_log.ro_id` is a UUID** (FK to `repair_orders.id`) — NOT the PRVS-XXXX-XXXX text id. This was miswritten in first-draft Q7 of `dupe_detection_queries.sql` (fixed Session 51). Double-check any new SQL that joins `audit_log`.
- **`time_logs.ro_id`** (not `repair_order_id`) — common source of "column does not exist" errors when writing new ad-hoc queries.
- Soft-delete UPDATE uses `.select()` + row-count assertion (`data.length === 0` → throw) so silent RLS rejections become loud errors. Pattern should be replicated on the 13 writes patched in v1.408 (GH#29c belt-and-suspenders — not yet done).

### Staff Offboarding Pattern (Session 54)
- **Reusable template for ANY terminated employee.** Scope touches 3 DB tables + Supabase Auth + external services. No code changes needed.
- **DB side (SQL, 3 statements):** (1) `UPDATE staff SET active=false, sms_opt_in_at=NULL, phone_number=NULL WHERE lower(email)='<email>'` — keeps the row so `buildRateByEmail()` in worklist-report can still compute historical labor cost from their `time_logs`. (2) `DELETE FROM user_roles WHERE user_id IN (SELECT id FROM users WHERE lower(email)='<email>')`. (3) `DELETE FROM users WHERE lower(email)='<email>'`.
- **Why NOT `DELETE FROM staff`:** `staff.hourly_rate` is load-bearing for historical labor-cost attribution. Deleting the row breaks every past `time_logs` labor rollup in worklist-report (renders as $0 for all of that person's past sessions). Inactivating is safer + reversible.
- **Why delete from `users` (not just clear user_roles):** `users` is the auth.users.id → email bridge. With the row gone, `loadUserRoles()` in index.html returns empty on any future login attempt → no role merge → no access. Belt-and-suspenders on top of Auth user deletion.
- **Supabase Auth side:** Dashboard → Authentication → Users → search email → "Sign out user" then "Delete user". Kills live sessions + prevents Google SSO re-login.
- **External services checklist:** Google Workspace (suspend/delete — this is the authoritative SSO cutoff), GitHub org (remove from PatriotsRV collaborators), Slack workspace, 1Password/shared-secret rotation.
- **NEVER delete:** `time_logs`, `audit_log`, `repair_orders.technician_assigned` — audit/payroll/historical integrity.
- **Verification queries:** `SELECT active FROM staff WHERE lower(email)=...` should show `false`. `SELECT * FROM users WHERE lower(email)=...` should return 0 rows. `SELECT ur.* FROM user_roles ur JOIN users u ON u.id=ur.user_id WHERE lower(u.email)=...` should return 0 rows.
- **Applied to:** Nik Polizzo (`nik@patriotsrvservices.com`) — Session 54, 2026-04-22. SQL delivered to Roland for execution; tracked as GH#35.
- **For future terminations:** copy the SQL block from GH#35 in the Active TODO List verbatim, swap the email.

### v1.408 UUID-First Lookup Fix (GH#29, Session 51)
- 13 write-path functions in index.html now use `ro._supabaseId ? findIndex(item._supabaseId === ro._supabaseId) : fallback(name+date)` to resolve `currentFilteredData[idx] → currentData`.
- **NEVER revert to the old `(customerName + dateReceived)` lookup** — dupes cause wrong-row writes. The fallback path exists for legacy data that predates `_supabaseId` population and should essentially never fire in practice (Supabase load at lines 10221/10339 always sets it).
- Functions affected: updateROStatus, updateROUrgency, updateROProgress, editField, uploadPhoto, uploadDocument, setMainPhoto, archiveRO, openScheduleModal, confirmSchedule, proceedWithSchedule, openPartsModal, openEditRO.
- If you add a new write-path that looks up an RO from `currentFilteredData`, use the UUID-first pattern from day one.

### CLAUDE_CONTEXT.md Storage (Session 29)
- **Local-primary strategy:** Read/write from `PRVS RO Dashboard` workspace folder. Push to GitHub at end of session as backup only.
- GitHub MCP tool has ~21KB content parameter limit — CLAUDE_CONTEXT.md is kept under this limit. CLAUDE_CONTEXT_HISTORY.md is local-primary; GitHub backup is best-effort.

### Autonomous Branch-Based Development Pattern (Session 64)
- **When Roland authorizes overnight/unattended work:** stage all changes on a feature branch (`wo-redesign`, etc.), open a PR to `main`, NEVER auto-merge. Roland reviews and merges in the morning. Reasoning: staff use `checkin.html` at 7am — a code regression with no human triage is unacceptable.
- **Sandbox network has TWO documented blockers** that any autonomous flow must work around:
  - **`api.github.com` returns `403 Forbidden`** to direct Python `urllib`/`requests` calls (HTTPS tunnel blocked at sandbox proxy). Workaround: use the GitHub MCP tools (`mcp__github__create_or_update_file`, `mcp__github__push_files`, `mcp__github__create_pull_request`, `mcp__github__create_branch`) which use a different egress path.
  - **`.git/HEAD.lock` is permanent** in the sandbox (`Operation not permitted` to remove). Any `git checkout` / `git switch` / `git checkout -b` fails. Workaround: use git plumbing that NEVER touches HEAD — `git fetch origin <branch>` (writes to `refs/remotes/`), `git hash-object -w <file>`, `git read-tree origin/<branch>` (writes to a TMP_INDEX, never .git/index), `git update-index --add --cacheinfo MODE,SHA,PATH`, `git write-tree`, `git commit-tree TREE -p PARENT`, `git push origin COMMIT_SHA:refs/heads/<branch>`. This sequence pushes a commit to a remote branch without ever changing local HEAD.
- **Every autonomous session must end with a clear `main`-untouched state.** PR awaits Roland; rollback is one revert click if anything goes wrong.
- **Spec-first discipline:** for any non-trivial feature, write the spec doc before the code. Roland reviews the spec; iteration on the spec is cheap. Iteration on code merged to main is expensive.
- **Judgment-call transparency:** every UX/design decision Claude makes without Roland gets explicitly listed in the PR body table. Roland overrides on review. Don't hide a decision in a comment somewhere — a one-row table item per choice.

## 🏗 Tech Stack

- **Frontend:** Vanilla JS (index/checkin/analytics); React 18.2.0 via CDN (solar.html)
- **Auth:** Google Identity Services (GIS) → Supabase `signInWithIdToken`
- **Database:** Supabase (PostgreSQL + RLS)
- **Storage:** Supabase Storage (`rv-media` bucket)
- **Backups:** GitHub Actions → `prvshepard/rv-dashboard-backups` (private), daily 4 AM EST
- **SMS:** Twilio (planned — full spec in `docs/specs/TWILIO_SMS_SPEC.md`, number port pending)
- **Offline:** IndexedDB queue in checkin.html
- **Hosting:** GitHub Pages

## 🗄 Supabase Tables

| Table | Purpose |
|---|---|
| `repair_orders` | Core RO data |
| `notes` | Append-only RO notes (type: `ro_status`, `customer_comm`) |
| `parts` | Parts per RO |
| `time_logs` | Technician time entries. **Session 52:** added `close_reason TEXT` column — `NULL` for normal tech-closed, `'auto_eod'` for closes by the 12h-cap pg_cron job. |
| `cashiered` | Cashiered/closed RO archive |
| `users` | User profiles |
| `user_roles` | User ↔ role join table |
| `roles` | Role definitions (Admin, Tech, Service Advisor, etc.) |
| `audit_log` | Field-level change audit trail |
| `config` | App configuration key/value store |
| `insurance_scans` | Insurance document scan data |
| `staff` | All PRVS personnel (name, email, role, service_silo, active). **Session 52:** added `hourly_rate NUMERIC(6,2) DEFAULT 0.00 NOT NULL`. `0.00` = tester, fully excluded from worklist-report surfaces. Migration: `supabase/migrations/staff_table.sql` + `supabase/migrations/add_staff_hourly_rate.sql`. |
| `service_work_orders` | One WO record per RO-silo combination |
| `service_tasks` | Individual task/step rows per WO. Includes `est_hours NUMERIC(5,2)` (added Session 30 via ALTER TABLE) |
| `wo_task_templates` | Saved WO task list templates per service silo (id, service_silo, template_name, created_by, updated_at) |
| `wo_template_tasks` | Individual task rows belonging to a template (template_id FK, task_title, description, est_hours, sort_order) |
| `manager_work_lists` | Manager personal RO work lists (id, manager_email, ro_id [UUID], ro_name, priority, created_at). RLS: each user manages own rows; Sr Managers/Admins can SELECT all rows. |
| `app_config` | App configuration key/value store (S7). Seeded with 8 calendar IDs. RLS: authenticated read, Admin write. `getCalendarId()` reads from here first, falls back to `CALENDAR_IDS_FALLBACK`. |
| `time_off_requests` | **GH#38 Phase 1 (Session 57).** Employee time off records. Columns: id UUID PK, employee_email TEXT, employee_name TEXT, start_date DATE, end_date DATE, request_type CHECK (sick/vacation/personal/general), notes TEXT (required reason field in UI), `total_days NUMERIC(5,2) GENERATED ALWAYS AS (end_date-start_date+1) STORED`, `partial_hours NUMERIC(4,1)` nullable (NULL = full day; 0.5–8.0 = partial-day hours; added Session 62 via `add_partial_hours_to_time_off.sql`), submitted_by_email TEXT, created_at TIMESTAMPTZ, updated_at TIMESTAMPTZ. Indexes on employee_email + date range. RLS: employees read-own, managers/admins read-all, authenticated insert, admin-only update/delete. |

## 🏛 Key Architecture Decisions

### Supabase RBAC
- RLS enabled on all 11 tables + storage bucket `rv-media`
- Helper function `has_role(role_name text)` — SECURITY DEFINER
- Pattern: `TO authenticated USING (true)` for reads; `WITH CHECK (has_role('Admin'))` for restricted writes
- **Status: ✅ Complete**

### Supabase Edge Function — roof-lookup
solar.html v2.0 calls `https://axfejhudchdejoiwaetq.supabase.co/functions/v1/roof-lookup` for AI roof dimension lookup. Code is committed but **must be deployed via CLI**:

```bash
npm install -g supabase
supabase login
supabase link --project-ref axfejhudchdejoiwaetq
supabase secrets set ANTHROPIC_API_KEY=sk-ant-...
supabase functions deploy roof-lookup
```

### ~~Supabase Edge Function — kenect-proxy~~ (REMOVED 2026-04-11)
Kenect refused to supply API keys. Edge Function deleted, all UI code removed. SMS/messaging migrating to Twilio.

### GH#18 Parts Notifications (Session 32)
- `requested_by_email` column on `repair_orders` — tracks who submitted the parts request. Set every time `submitPartsRequest()` is called (most recent requester).
- `updated_at` column on `parts` — auto-stamp trigger `_prvs_set_updated_at()`. Both columns added via `gh18_migration.sql` (Roland must run in Supabase SQL Editor — NOT yet run as of session 32).
- `notifyPartsRequester(filteredIndex)` — manual trigger from Parts Status modal. Shows confirm dialog with parts list preview. Only shown when `ro.requestedByEmail` is set. POSTs to `send-quote-email` with type `'parts_ordered'`.
- `notifyPartsEtaUpdate(ro, partName, eta)` — non-blocking auto-fire from `savePartForm` when ETA is set/changed on edit, or when ETA is set on a newly-added part. Only fires if `requestedByEmail` is set on the RO.
- `send-parts-report` Edge Function needs Supabase CLI deploy: `supabase functions deploy send-parts-report`. Uses SUPABASE_SERVICE_ROLE_KEY (built-in env var) + GMAIL_USER + GMAIL_APP_PASSWORD secrets.
- `parts-report.yml` cron uses `SUPABASE_SERVICE_ROLE_KEY` GitHub secret (different name from backup.yml which uses `SUPABASE_SERVICE_KEY`). Check existing secrets in GitHub → Settings → Secrets before adding.
- ⚠️ The `parts` table FK to `repair_orders` is the **`ro_id`** column (UUID) — NOT `repair_order_id`. Confirmed from `appendPartToSupabase()` in index.html. Any Supabase query filtering parts by RO must use `.in("ro_id", ...)` or `.eq("ro_id", ...)`. The Supabase join syntax is `.select("..., repair_orders(ro_id, customer_name, rv)")`. The `send-parts-report` openROPartsMap query had this wrong (used `repair_order_id`) — fixed Session 32. **Session 37: same bug found in sections 2/3/4 (ordered, overdue, received queries) — all three still used `repair_order_id`. Fixed + redeployed.**

### Daily Backup
- `.github/workflows/backup.yml` — 8 AM UTC (4 AM EST) daily + manual trigger
- Exports all 11 tables via Supabase REST API (service role key)
- Pushes to private repo `prvshepard/rv-dashboard-backups`, rolling 30-day retention
- Required secrets: `SUPABASE_URL`, `SUPABASE_SERVICE_KEY`, `GH_BACKUP_PAT`
- **Status: ✅ Live and tested**

The extractor happily reported 1,486 files at 7-8 MB/s while Storage held only **200 objects** — it was re-downloading the same 200 forever (tell: `attempts` pinned at exactly the 200-row page size; proof: PATCH with `Prefer: count=exact` → `Content-Range: */0`). Fixed with a SECURITY DEFINER RPC that RETURNS the row count + asserts it. Same root cause killed PostgREST upsert (**both** merge-duplicates AND ignore-duplicates → 42501) and Storage `x-upsert` ⇒ **plain INSERT only**; checkpointing comes from the MCP read side. **MEDIA DECISION REVISED ON REAL DATA:** Phase 0's '2-7 GB' came from ONE unrepresentative 576 KB PDF sample; true avg ~3 MB ⇒ **~50-100 GB**, with just **78 video files @ ~27 MB ≈ half the volume** — Roland re-asked and chose **PDFs + images, SKIP VIDEO** (608 video files / 8 GB skipped), enforced in SQL by the worklist view, not extractor logic. That turned a ~50-hr job into ~1 hr. Concurrency was decisive: 4 workers = 0.26 MB/s vs 16 workers = ~11 MB/s. **VERIFIED:** md5 **7,754/7,756 exact** (the 2 'mismatches' are multipart eTags `<md5ofmd5s>-2` on a 17.4 MB image, sizes match exactly ⇒ ZERO corruption); **live spot-check 12/12 MATCH** incl. the deepest thread at **2,087 msgs** (spec assumed 327 — paging to exhaustion was load-bearing); Storage bytes == sum of Kenect-reported sizes exactly. **TEARDOWN DONE + empirically re-tested from the browser with the public anon key: insert 401 / upload 400 / RPC 401 all blocked; reads still `[]`; authenticated policies kept so Phase 4 is unblocked.** Teardown initially FAILED because `DELETE FROM storage.objects` is blocked by `storage.protect_delete()` and the SQL editor's one-transaction behaviour rolled back the ENTIRE script (verified nothing applied, then removed the line). **🔴 PHASE 4 TARGET CORRECTED — the spec was written against a schema that doesn't exist:** `conversation_events` is an AUDIT table (no body/direction/media) so messages CANNOT go there; they belong in **`public.messages`**; `conversations` has NO `source` column; messages link to threads **BY PHONE ONLY, no FK**; and `messages` has **no external-id unique constraint** ⇒ add `kenect_message_id bigint unique` BEFORE Phase 4 or the delta WILL duplicate. **NOT DONE:** Phase 4 transform (deliberately deferred — extraction was the time-critical part; raw data is now permanent) and the **7/21 delta pull**.
